tricks guide 
---------------------------------------------------
seatstand: l r d t   bunnyhop: u u t   no footer: u d t
skysurf
360: l r d t   roll: r r t   helicopter: u d u t
bungeejump
twist: d d d t   spiral: l r l t   somersault: u d u t
mountain bike
no footer: d u t   360: l r t   backflip: l u d t
speedglide
roll: r r t   somersault: d d u t   dip: u d u t
l: left  r: right  d: down  u: up  t: trick button
